With the Food Storage Emergency All-in-One 6 Gallon Pail you&#39;re not only getting a reserve supply of food, you&#39;re getting delicious peace of mind.
&lt;p&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

The included 30-Day Meal Planner offers a wide range of appetizing combinations, making it easy to mix and match meals. If you&rsquo;re looking to extend the number of days the meals will last, a 45-day meal planner with a lower calorie per day average is also included.

&lt;p&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;
Augason Farms knows storing combustible fuel poses many risks. FireOn is a secure alternative, designed as an emergency fire starter. It is a safe, non-combustible, burnable material that lights quickly in even adverse conditions. FireOn takes the guesswork out of how to cook food or stay warm in an emergency.

&lt;p&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

		}else if(location.pathname.indexOf('cart.jsp')&gt;-1){
			oGoogleDFP.path = '/cart';
		}else if(location.pathname.indexOf('homepage.jsp')&gt;-1 || location.href == 'http://www.samsclub.com/sams/'){
			oGoogleDFP.path = '/Homepage';
			oGoogleDFP.page = 'main';
		}else if(location.pathname.indexOf('searchResults.jsp')&gt;-1){
			oGoogleDFP.page = 'searchresults';
		}else if(location.pathname.indexOf('.ip')&gt;-1 || location.pathname.indexOf('.cp')&gt;-1){
			oGoogleDFP.path = oGoogleDFP.path.split('/').slice(1); //remove All_Products
			if(location.pathname.indexOf('.ip')&gt;-1) oGoogleDFP.path.pop(); //remove product
			oGoogleDFP.path = (oGoogleDFP.path.length &gt; 4)? '/'+oGoogleDFP.path.slice(0,4).join('/') : '/'+oGoogleDFP.path.join('/');
			oGoogleDFP.page = (location.pathname.indexOf('.ip')&gt;-1)? 'product' : 'main';
		}else if(location.pathname.indexOf('content.jsp')&gt;-1){
			if(location.search.indexOf('pageName=')&gt;-1) oGoogleDFP.path = '/Seasonal/'+location.search.split('pageName=')[1].split('&amp;')[0];
			oGoogleDFP.page = 'seasonal';
		}
		if(location.search.indexOf('searchTerm=')&gt;-1) oGoogleDFP.search = location.search.split('searchTerm=')[1].split('&amp;')[0];
		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			googletag.defineSlot('/41919049/SamsClub-US'+oGoogleDFP.path, [[1000, 25], [1000, 300]], 'expandableAd').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting('page',oGoogleDFP.page).setTargeting('search',oGoogleDFP.search);
			googletag.defineSlot('/41919049/SamsClub-US'+oGoogleDFP.path, [[728, 90]], 'leaderboardTopAd').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting('page',oGoogleDFP.page).setTargeting('pos','Top').setTargeting('search',oGoogleDFP.search);
			googletag.defineSlot('/41919049/SamsClub-US'+oGoogleDFP.path, [[728, 90]], 'leaderboardBottomAd').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting('page',oGoogleDFP.page).setTargeting('pos','Bottom').setTargeting('search',oGoogleDFP.search);
			googletag.defineSlot('/41919049/SamsClub-US'+oGoogleDFP.path, [[160, 600]], 'skyscraperAd').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting('page',oGoogleDFP.page).setTargeting('search',oGoogleDFP.search);
			googletag.defineSlot('/41919049/SamsClub-US'+oGoogleDFP.path, [[300, 250]], 'rectangleAd').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting('page',oGoogleDFP.page).setTargeting('search',oGoogleDFP.search);
			googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();
			googletag.pubads().setTargeting("samsVisitor", getSamsVisitorCookie ("samsVisitor"));
			googletag.enableServices();
		});
  </script>
  <!-- R 13.9 : get the bread crumb in header for google Ad -End-->

        <script type="text/javascript">
         head.ready(function(){
	var bvapiUrl = window.location.protocol + "//samsclub.ugc.bazaarvoice.com/static/1337/bvapi.js";
			window.loadBazaarvoiceApi = function(callback) {
			if (window.$BV) {
				callback();
				} else {
				$.getScript(bvapiUrl, function() {
					$($BV.docReady);
						callback();
						});
				}
			};
	loadBazaarvoiceApi(function() {	
		$BV.configure("global", {
			submissionContainerUrl: "http://www.samsclub.com/sams/common/reviewsubmission.jsp"
		});
	});
	
	loadBazaarvoiceApi(function() {	
		$BV.ui("rr", "show_reviews", {productId: "prod5610448",onEvent: function(json) {
						
					var totalReviewsCount = json.attributes.numReviews;
					var avgRating = json.attributes.avgRating;
					var ratingsOnlyReviewCount = json.attributes.numRatingsOnlyReviews;
					var recommendPercentage = json.attributes.percentRecommend;
					var productID = json.productId;
					if (json.eventSource == "Display") {
						// Other custom items leveraging these values.
						omnitureReview=new Object();
						var bvo=omnitureReview; 
						bvo.totalReviewCount=totalReviewsCount;
						bvo.avgRating=avgRating;
						bvo.totalRatingOnlyCount=ratingsOnlyReviewCount;
						bvo.buyAgainPercentage=buyAgainPercentage;
						bvo.product=productID;
						bvo.reviewsFound=1;
							 if(typeof(s)!='undefined')
							{
						    bvo.omtr_products=s.products;
							var ltv=s.linkTrackVars;bvo.ajaxCatch=1;
							s.tl(true,'o','BazaarVoice Catch');
							s.linkTrackVars=ltv;
							}
			     }
			   }
			});
	});

	loadBazaarvoiceApi(function() {	
		$BV.ui("qa", "show_questions", {productId: "prod5610448", subjectType: "product"});
	});
	});

           var RRSessionID = {'currentProductSessionID' :''}
function getCurrentSessionID() {
    var name = 'JSESSIONID', nameEQ = name + "=", ca = document.cookie.split(';'), c;
    for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
      c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
      if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) === 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
    return null;
  }
RRSessionID.currentProductSessionID = getCurrentSessionID();
	var R3_COMMON = new r3_common();
	R3_COMMON.setApiKey('8791bbd765435838');
	R3_COMMON.setBaseUrl('http://recs.richrelevance.com/rrserver/');
	R3_COMMON.setSessionId(RRSessionID.currentProductSessionID);
	R3_COMMON.setUserId('6424557207');
    
        R3_COMMON.addClickthruParams(0,'campaign_data=prod5610448');

             <h2>
              About this item
             </h2>
             <div class="clearfix">
             </div>
             <!-- Start Panel :About this Item  -->
             <div class="tab-pane span8 offset0" id="panelAboutItem">
              <!--Short Description -->
              <div class="itemBullets span7 offset0 pull-left ft14 gray6">
               <ul>
                <li>
                 1 Person
                </li>
                <li>
                 300 Total Servings
                </li>
                <li>
                 1,857 Average Calories per day
                </li>
                <li>
                 1 Pail with 8 Mylar Food pouches
                </li>
                <li>
                 1 Fire starter disk
                </li>
                <li>
                 1 Water bottle with Filter
                </li>
               </ul>
              </div>
              <!--End of Short Description -->
              <div class="clearfix">
              </div>
              <!-- SEO semantic mark up start - added itemprop  -->
              <div class="itemDescription span8 offset0">
               <!-- Long Description  -->
               <h3>
                Description
               </h3>
               <span itemprop="description">
                <p class="ft14 itemDetailsPara">
                </p>
                <div class="content_style">
                 <a href="http://video.samsclub.com/mediaroom/?id=1579&amp;popupView=1" onclick="window.open('http://video.samsclub.com/mediaroom/?id=1579&amp;popupView=1','_blank', 'toolbar=no,location=no,directories=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,top=0,left=0,width=437, height=360'); return false;">
                  View a video of this product
                 </a>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 Augason Farms 30-Day Food Storage Emergency All-in-One Pail is your survival solution. This waterproof pail contains enough food to provide 1,857 calories per day for 1 person for a month, or a family of 4 for a week. The pail also includes a safe, stable fuel source and a self-filtering water bottle that can clean up to 100 gallons of water. With the Food Storage Emergency All-in-One 6 Gallon Pail you're not only getting a reserve supply of food, you're getting delicious peace of mind.
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 Augason Farms crafts their food for both everyday and food storage use. You can rest assured that your family will love their tried and true recipes. Whether it's a hearty oatmeal breakfast or filling cheesy broccoli rice, these foods are easy to prepare and have home cooked flavor. The included 30-Day Meal Planner offers a wide range of appetizing combinations, making it easy to mix and match meals. If youre looking to extend the number of days the meals will last, a 45-day meal planner with a lower calorie per day average is also included.
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 The self-filtering water bottle removes up to 99.99% of bacteria, viruses, contaminants and pollutants. The filtering bottle is simple to use. Just pop the top, fill the bottle, and let the Miraguard filter do the rest.
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 Augason Farms knows storing combustible fuel poses many risks. FireOn is a secure alternative, designed as an emergency fire starter. It is a safe, non-combustible, burnable material that lights quickly in even adverse conditions. FireOn takes the guesswork out of how to cook food or stay warm in an emergency.
                 <p>
                 </p>
                 Items sealed in the 30-Day Food Storage Emergency All-in-One Pail have a shelf life up to 20 years. Great for cabins, boats, and even to put in your vehicle. Family owned and operated since 1972, you can trust Augason Farms' proven shelf life because they have outlived their guarantees and then some.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <a class="mainstay-lk52" href="http://scene7.samsclub.com/is/content/samsclub/38280_nutEpdf" target="_blank">
                  View nutrition information here.
                 </a>
                 (PDF)
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <a class="mainstay-lk52" href="http://scene7.samsclub.com/is/content/samsclub/38280_Menupdf" target="_blank">
                  View menu planner here.
                 </a>
                 (PDF)
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 Looking for the right kit for you? Compare Augason Farms kits
                 <a class="mainstay-lk52" href="http://scene7.samsclub.com/is/content/samsclub/Kitcomp4-13revpdf" target="_blank">
                  here.
                 </a>
                 (PDF)

              <!-- Item Features  -->
              <div class="itemFeatures span8 offset0 itemDetailsPara">
               <h3>
                Specifications
               </h3>
               <p>
               </p>
               <div class="content_style">
                Augason Farms 30-Day Food Storage Emergency All-in-One Pail  components proudly made in the USA
                <ul>
                 <li>
                  Pail contains 300 servings providing and average of 1,857 calories per day
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Each delicious meal takes 20 minutes or less to prepare  just add water
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  No high fructose corn syrup, trans fats or MSG
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Up to 20 year shelf life sealed; pouch life up to 1 year after opening*
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Easy to use self-filtering water bottle  filters up to 100 gallons
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  1 FireOn disk in each pail, large enough to break apart for multiple uses
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  30-day meal planner, plus extended 45-day meal planner included
                 </li>
                </ul>
                Eight great-tasting food varieties in re-sealable Mylar bags with oxygen absorbers
                <ul>
                 <li>
                  Instant Potatoes  30 servings
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Macaroni and Cheese  30 servings
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Creamy Potato Soup  30 servings
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Cheesy Broccoli Rice  30 servings
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Creamy Chicken Rice  30 servings
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Hearty Vegetable Blend  30 servings
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Maple Brown Sugar Oatmeal  40 servings
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  Morning Moos Low Fat Milk Alternative  80 servings
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <p>
                 Self-filtering water bottle with microbiological filter:
                 <br/>
                 Clean, fresh water wherever you go with this all-in-one solution. 24-ounce plastic water bottle with pull-top cap fits in a back pocket, backpack, or in your bike bottle holder. Just fill from any water source (except salt water) and the included filter provides clean water as you drink, removing sediment, contaminants, and other pathogens. The Ionic Adsorption Micron Filtration System is good for up to 100 gallons of filtered water.
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 FireOn Emergency Fuel-Heat Source-Fire Starter Easy to use as a fire starter or a sole heat source. Effortlessly started with a match, the intact disk will burn for up to 30 minutes. Since most meals require only about 15 minutes cooking time on a small, portable camp stove, FireOn can be extinguished and re-lit or broken in half for dual use. Add to any fuel source to start your fire .
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <i>
                  *Best when stored in a cool, dry place at temperatures between 50F and 70F (ideal humidity 15%)
                 </i>
                </p>
               </div>
